# V4.2 overtrading hell

> *Raw extractions of cognitive dissonance and market-induced panic.* 

---

### 🤯 Breakdown: 601869.SH on 2024-12-03 (Action: WAIT)

**Brief Rationale (What the bosses see):**
> No position. Trend just started yesterday but already in pullback mode (trend_mode=pullback). 60-min shows RANGE regime with ZS Stack Count=0 and no BSP entry signal. RSI declining from 55.2 to 53.7 shows mild weakness. ADX>34 with DI+>DI- confirms trend existence but lack of entry timing signal means I should wait. Rule 6 (Breakdown Veto) cautions against buying into pullbacks. I will wait for either (1) 60-min BSP buy signal, or (2) trend_mode shifts to acceleration/mature_trend with price confirmation.

**Inner Journal (What she is actually screaming inside):**
> Discipline check: I see ADX 34.6 and DI+ > DI- and my instinct is to jump in. But the trend_mode is literally 'pullback' and 60-min shows RANGE with zero ZS stack. This is not a fat pitch. It's a maybe-trend that just started yesterday and already pulled back. I've been burned too many times buying into the first pullback of a new trend, only to watch it chop sideways for weeks. My job is to swing at fat pitches, not guess on marginal setups. I'll wait for the 60-min to give me a BSP buy signal, or wait for the pullback to resolve and trend_mode to shift to acceleration. Cash is a position too. I'm not missing anything by waiting for confirmation. If this is a real trend, it will give me multiple entry points over the coming weeks.

---

I know Rule 1 says 'when ADX > 35, RSI > 70 is trend strength not overbought' - but ADX is 31.5, not 35 yet, and RSI is 51.2. This isn't a Rule 1 situation. This is me being impatient. I'll wait for either a pullback to 26-27 OR a clear BSP buy signal. Cash is a position too.
